/* 1. Write a query to count how many records there are in your table. */

mysql> SELECT COUNT(*) FROM music;
+----------+
| COUNT(*) |
+----------+
|     4681 |
+----------+
1 row in set (0.01 sec)

/* Deleting the Header Row */

mysql> DELETE 
    -> FROM music
    -> WHERE artist = "artist";
Query OK, 1 row affected (0.01 sec)

mysql> SELECT COUNT(*) FROM music;
+----------+
| COUNT(*) |
+----------+
|     4680 |
+----------+
1 row in set (0.01 sec)

/* 2. Write a query to logically group the data in your table and print out only the last (or highest) record in each category. */

mysql> SELECT song, year_written, artist FROM music ORDER BY artist DESC LIMIT 1;
+---------------------------+--------------+---------+
| song                      | year_written | artist  |
+---------------------------+--------------+---------+
| Wraparound Shades (Album) |         1995 | Zumpano |
+---------------------------+--------------+---------+
1 row in set (0.01 sec)

/* 3. Display three important fields; at least one should be in alphabetical order; show only the first 10 records in the table. */

/* 4. Use GROUP BY to find averages on a numerical field in a reasonable breakdown. */

mysql> SELECT artist, REPLACE(FORMAT(AVG(year_written),0),",","") AS AverageYearForHitSong  FROM music GROUP BY artist;

/* 5. Create a user-friendly listing of the first 15 records in alphabetical order. */

mysql> SELECT CONCAT(artist," (",song,",",year_written,")") as Hit_Song FROM music ORDER BY artist LIMIT 15;
+--------------------------------------------------------------+
| Hit_Song                                                     |
+--------------------------------------------------------------+

/* 7. Number of Songs in the Dataset for each Artist */

/* Artists with greater than or equal to 10 songs in the dataset in Alphabetical */

mysql> SELECT artist,COUNT(song) AS NumberOfSongs FROM music GROUP BY artist HAVING COUNT(song) >= 10 LIMIT 10;

/* 10. Using CONCAT, OR, and LIKE to find the songs (with Track_ID) of Pearl Jam and RHCP */

mysql> SELECT CONCAT(song," (",track_id,")") AS SongWithTrack_ID,artist,year_written FROM music WHERE artist="Red hot chili peppers" OR artist = "pearl Jam" ORDER BY artist,year_written;
+---------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------+--------------+

| American Ghost Dance (2003 Digital Remas (TRAJBJG128F14A1EA1) | Red Hot Chili Peppers |         1985 |

/* 11. Seeing the two oldest and newest songs in the dataset  */

mysql> SELECT year_written,song FROM music ORDER BY year_written LIMIT 2;
+--------------+---------------------+
| year_written | song                |
+--------------+---------------------+
|         1926 | Long Lonesome Blues |
|         1926 | Got The Blues       |
+--------------+---------------------+
2 rows in set (0.01 sec)

mysql> SELECT year_written,song FROM music ORDER BY year_written DESC LIMIT 2;
+--------------+------------------------------------------+
| year_written | song                                     |
+--------------+------------------------------------------+
|         2010 | Rette Mich Spter (Michael Ilbert Radio M |
|         2010 | The Doug McComb Over                     |
+--------------+------------------------------------------+
2 rows in set (0.00 sec)

/* 12. The average year in the dataset for the songs */

mysql> SELECT REPLACE(FORMAT(AVG(year_written),0),",","") AS AverageYearForHitSong  FROM music;
+-----------------------+
| AverageYearForHitSong |
+-----------------------+
| 1997                  |
+-----------------------+
1 row in set (0.00 sec)
